======================================================================
STARTUP RENDERER RESOURCE AUDIT
======================================================================
Goal:
  Identify concrete GPU/resource creation paths that can explain the
  startup renderer bucket, and list hook/patch surfaces used by NVR and Stewie.

Source hints:
  NVR attaches InitializeRenderer, shader creation, SetShaderPackage,
  Render, image-space, scene-graph, first-person, and sampler-state hooks.
  Stewie skips texture/VB zeroing at 0x00E68BA9 and 0x00E8C051.
